  DATASET

    { 1100525000;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012021;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               FormatAddress.Company(CompanyAddr, CompanyInformation);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  TempVATAmountLine.DELETEALL;

                                  CLEAR(AmountSSExc);
                                  CLEAR(AmountSSInc);
                                  CLEAR(AmountSSIncVAT);
                                  CLEAR(AmountCTExc);
                                  CLEAR(AmountCTInc);

                                  IF "Project No." <> Job."No." THEN BEGIN
                                    CLEAR(ProjectAddr);
                                    Job.GET("Project No.");
                                    FormatAddress.Project(ProjectAddr, Job);
                                  END;

                                  IF Principal <> Customer."No." THEN BEGIN
                                    Customer.GET(Principal);
                                    IF Customer."Currency Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                      Currency.GET(Customer."Currency Code");
                                      Currency.TESTFIELD("Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
                                      Currency.TESTFIELD("Amount Rounding Precision");
                                      IF Customer."Currency Code" <> GeneralLedgerSetup."LCY Code" THEN
                                        CurrencyFactor := CurrencyExchangeRate.ExchangeRate(
                                          0,'', WORKDATE, Customer."Currency Code", TRUE)
                                      ELSE
                                        CurrencyFactor := 0;
                                      TotalTextExclSurcharge := STRSUBSTNO(Text000, Customer."Currency Code");
                                      TotalText := STRSUBSTNO(Text001, Customer."Currency Code");
                                      TotalInclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text002, Customer."Currency Code");
                                      AmountRoundPrecision := Currency."Amount Rounding Precision";
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      CurrencyFactor := 0;
                                      TotalTextExclSurcharge := STRSUBSTNO(Text000, GeneralLedgerSetup."LCY Code");
                                      TotalText := STRSUBSTNO(Text001, GeneralLedgerSetup."LCY Code");
                                      TotalInclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text002, GeneralLedgerSetup."LCY Code");
                                      AmountRoundPrecision := GeneralLedgerSetup."Amount Rounding Precision";
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF ("Project No." <> ProjectPrincipal."Project No.") OR
                                     (Principal <> ProjectPrincipal.Principal)
                                  THEN BEGIN
                                    CLEAR(CustomerAddr);
                                    ProjectPrincipal.GET("Project No.", Principal);
                                    ProjectPrincipal.CALCFIELDS("Contact Person Name");
                                    IF ProjectPrincipal."Alternative Bill-to Address" = '' THEN BEGIN
                                      FormatAddress.Customer(CustomerAddr, Customer);
                                    END ELSE
                                      IF ShiptoAddress.GET(Principal, ProjectPrincipal."Alternative Bill-to Address") THEN
                                        FormatAddress.Address(CustomerAddr, ShiptoAddress);
                                  END;

                                  Commission.GET("Project No.", Principal, "Commission No.");
                                  Commission.CALCFIELDS("Supervisor Name");
                                  IF NOT Employee.GET(Job."Site Manager") THEN
                                    Employee.INIT;
                                END;
                                 }

               DataItemTable=Table11012019;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Project No.,Principal,Commission No.,Settl.Sheet No.,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Chargeable=CONST(Yes));
               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  "Sales Amount (LCY)" := GetSalesAmount();
                                  BasicAmount := GetBasicAmount();
                                  ProcessCostPlusEntries(Quantity, "Basic Price (LCY)", BasicAmount, "Sales Price (LCY)", "Sales Amount (LCY)", "VAT Prod. Posting Group");

                                  PrintEmployee := FALSE;
                                  IF ("Cost Type" = "Cost Type"::Labor) AND ("Employee No." <> '') OR ("From Date" <> 0D) OR ("To Date" <> 0D) THEN BEGIN
                                    PrintEmployee := TRUE;

                                    IF NOT Employee2.GET("Employee No.") THEN
                                      Employee2.INIT;

                                    PeriodTxt := '';
                                    IF "From Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      PeriodTxt := STRSUBSTNO('%1', "From Date");

                                    IF ("To Date" <> 0D) AND ("To Date" <> "From Date") THEN
                                      PeriodTxt := STRSUBSTNO(Text004, PeriodTxt, "To Date");

                                    SocSecNoTxt := '';
                                    //Employee.CALCFIELDS("Social Security No.");
                                    IF Employee."Social Security No." <> '' THEN
                                      SocSecNoTxt := STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', Employee.FIELDCAPTION("Social Security No."), Employee."Social Security No.");
                                  END;

                                  SurchDisc:=0;
                                  IF "Project Cost Plus Entry"."Sales Discount % (Item)"<>0 THEN
                                   SurchDisc:="Project Cost Plus Entry"."Sales Discount % (Item)"*-1
                                  ELSE IF "Project Cost Plus Entry"."Surcharge %"<>0 THEN
                                    SurchDisc:="Project Cost Plus Entry"."Surcharge %";

                                  DescWage:='';
                                  CALCFIELDS("Project Cost Plus Entry"."Description Wage Component");
                                  IF "Project Cost Plus Entry"."Description Wage Component"<>'' THEN
                                    DescWage:='-'+"Project Cost Plus Entry"."Description Wage Component";
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Settlement Sheet;
               DataItemLink=Project No.=FIELD(Project No.),
                            Principal=FIELD(Principal),
                            Commission No.=FIELD(Commission No.),
                            Settl.Sheet No.=FIELD(No.) }

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE ProcessCostPlusEntries@16(Quantity@11012000 : Decimal;VAR "Unit Cost"@11012001 : Decimal;VAR "Unit Amount"@1210190000 : Decimal;VAR "Sales Price"@11012002 : Decimal;VAR "Sales Amount"@1210190001 : Decimal;"VAT Prod. Posting Group"@11012003 : Code[10]);
    BEGIN
      //Convert Unit Price & Amount into Customer Currency
      IF Customer."Currency Code" <> GeneralLedgerSetup."LCY Code" THEN BEGIN
        "Unit Cost" :=
          ROUND
            (CurrencyExchangeRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
              0,'', WORKDATE, Customer."Currency Code",
              "Unit Cost", CurrencyFactor, TRUE),
              Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
        "Unit Amount" :=
          ROUND
            (CurrencyExchangeRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
              0,'', WORKDATE, Customer."Currency Code",
              "Unit Amount", CurrencyFactor, TRUE),
              Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      END;

      //Convert Sales Price & Amount to Custumer Currency
      IF Customer."Currency Code" <> GeneralLedgerSetup."LCY Code" THEN BEGIN
        "Sales Price" :=
          ROUND
            (CurrencyExchangeRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
              0,'', WORKDATE, Customer."Currency Code",
              "Sales Price", CurrencyFactor, TRUE),
              Currency."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision");
        "Sales Amount" :=
          ROUND
            (CurrencyExchangeRate.ExchangeAmtLCYToFCY(
              0,'', WORKDATE, Customer."Currency Code",
              "Sales Amount", CurrencyFactor, TRUE),
              Currency."Amount Rounding Precision");
      END;

      //Calculate and Round Amounts per Settlement Sheet
      "Project Cost Plus Entry".CALCFIELDS("Cost Type");
      AmountExc := ROUND("Unit Amount", AmountRoundPrecision);
      AmountInc := ROUND("Sales Amount", AmountRoundPrecision);

      AmountCTExc["Project Cost Plus Entry"."Cost Type" + 1] := AmountCTExc["Project Cost Plus Entry"."Cost Type" + 1] + AmountExc;
      AmountCTInc["Project Cost Plus Entry"."Cost Type" + 1] := AmountCTInc["Project Cost Plus Entry"."Cost Type" + 1] + AmountInc;
      AmountSSExc := AmountSSExc + AmountExc;
      AmountSSInc := AmountSSInc + AmountInc;

      //VAT
      IF (ProjectPrincipal."VAT Bus. Posting Group" <> '') THEN BEGIN
        IF NOT VATPostingSetup.GET(ProjectPrincipal."VAT Bus. Posting Group", "VAT Prod. Posting Group") THEN
          VATPostingSetup.INIT;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF NOT VATPostingSetup.GET(Job."VAT Bus. Posting Group", "VAT Prod. Posting Group") THEN
          VATPostingSetup.INIT;
      END;
      VATPerc := VATPostingSetup."VAT %";
      CASE VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type" OF
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT",
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
          VATPerc := 0;
      END;

      CASE VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type" OF
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Normal VAT",
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
          BEGIN
            VATBase := AmountInc;
            AmountIncVAT := ROUND(AmountInc + VATBase * VATPerc / 100, 0.00001);
          END;
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT":
          BEGIN
            VATBase := 0;
            AmountIncVAT := AmountInc;
          END;
        VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
      //  Voorlopig niet ondersteund. Is alleen van toepassing op de Amerikaanse markt
          BEGIN
            VATBase := AmountInc;
            AmountIncVAT := AmountInc;
          END;
      END;

      AmountSSIncVAT := AmountSSIncVAT + AmountIncVAT;

      TempVATAmountLine.INIT;
      TempVATAmountLine."VAT Identifier" := VATPostingSetup."VAT Identifier";
      TempVATAmountLine."VAT Calculation Type" := VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type";
      TempVATAmountLine."VAT %" := VATPerc;
      TempVATAmountLine."VAT Base" := VATBase;
      TempVATAmountLine."Amount Including VAT" := AmountIncVAT;
      TempVATAmountLine.InsertLine;

      PrintTotal := TRUE;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      161006 ITERO.FH IME492 Changed Norwegian captionML
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value = 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Shared offset As Integer
Shared newgroup As Object
Shared currentgroup1 As Object
Shared currentgroup2 As Object
Shared currentgroup3 As Object
Shared currentgroup4 As Object

Public Function GetGroupPageNumber(newgroup2 As Boolean, pagenumber As Integer) As Object
    If newgroup2
        offset = pagenumber - 1
    End If
    Return pagenumber - offset
End Function

Public Function InNewGroup(group1 As Object, group2 As Object, group3 As Object, group4 As Object) As Boolean
    newgroup = False
    If Not (group1 = currentgroup1)
        newgroup = True
        currentgroup4 = group4
        currentgroup3 = group3
        currentgroup2 = group2
        currentgroup1 = group1
    Else
        If Not (group2 = currentgroup2)
            newgroup = True
            currentgroup4 = group4
            currentgroup3 = group3
            currentgroup2 = group2
        Else
            If Not (group3 = currentgroup3)
                newgroup = True
                currentgroup4 = group4
                currentgroup3 = group3
            Else
                If Not (group4 = currentgroup4)
                    newgroup = True
                    currentgroup4 = group4
                End If
            End If
        End If
    End If
    Return newgroup
End Function

Shared Data1 As Object

Public Function GetData(Num As Integer) As Object
    Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1), Chr(177))))
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData As Object)
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data1 = NewData
    End If
End Function
